                <h3 class="gfxhead">
                 <a class="gfxhead" href="https://www.chicagobusiness.com/news/tracking-coronavirus-illinois">
                  Tracking COVID-19
                 </a>
                </h3>
                <p class="introtext">
                 As of Nov. 6, probable cases (including positive antigen tests and cases that meet clinical criteria but are not yet confirmed) are being included in the state's confirmed COVID-19 case count. Follow all of Crain's COVID-19 coverage
                 <a class="introtext linkcolor" href="https://www.chicagobusiness.com/topic/coronavirus">
                  <strong>
                   here.
                  </strong>
                 </a>
                 For even more data, check out Crain's
                 <a class="introtext linkcolor" href="https://www.chicagobusiness.com/news/tracking-coronavirus-illinois">
                  <strong>
                   COVID-19 vaccine and case tracker.
                  </strong>
                 </a>
                 Also, don't miss the visualization
                 <a class="introtext linkcolor" href="https://www.chicagobusiness.com/health-care/when-can-we-get-back-business-usual">
                  <strong>
                   Getting Back To Business As Usual
                  </strong>
                 </a>
                 to see just when we might hit 'herd immunity.'
                </p>
                <iframe allowfullscreen="" class="cpsFrame" frameborder="0" mozallowfullscreen="" src="https://crain-platform-ccb-assets.s3.amazonaws.com/assets/interactive/coronavirus/covid19-homepage/covid-snapshot-with-vaccines.html" webkitallowfullscreen="" width="100%">
                </iframe>
               </div>
               <div class="fullchart makewider makewideradjust">
                <h3 class="gfxsubhead">

                  Track the Illinois vaccine rollout
                 </a>
                </h3>
                <a href="https://www.chicagobusiness.com/news/tracking-coronavirus-illinois">
                 <img id="vaccineReferImage" src="https://s3-prod.chicagobusiness.com/vaccine-tracker-image-map.jpg"/>
                </a>
               </div>
               <div class="fullchart makewider">
                <h3 class="gfxsubhead">

                       The state House passed the measure yesterday, aiming to eliminate a barrier to renting for people who have lost income during the pandemic.
                      </p>
                     </a>
